# Queries Visualization Properties
1710

NL Queries:

  1. A bar chart for finding the number of the country of the airlines whose name starts with 'Orbit', and sort country in desc order.

  2. A bar chart for what are the number of the countries of all airlines whose names start with Orbit?, sort from high to low by the names.

  3. What are the number of the countries of all airlines whose names start with Orbit?, and I want to sort in descending by the bars.

  4. What are the countries of all airlines whose names start with Orbit, and count them by a bar chart, sort bars in desc order.

  5. Find the country of the airlines whose name starts with 'Orbit', and count them by a bar chart, could you rank by the x axis from high to low?

  6. Find the number of the country of the airlines whose name starts with 'Orbit', and sort from high to low by the names.

VIS Query:

Visualize BAR SELECT country , COUNT(country) FROM airlines WHERE name LIKE 'Orbit%' GROUP BY country ORDER BY country DESC

(NL, VIS) ID: 1419@x_name@DESC

Hardness: Extra Hard

Chart: Bar

DB: flight_4
